         <script>
          window.is_valid_starbucks = function() {
        var is_valid = false;
        var valid_duration = 1; //in hours
        var remaining_time;
        var now = new Date();
        if ('undefined' !== typeof(Storage)) {
            var rj_starbucks_date = localStorage.getItem('rj_starbucks_date');
            if (rj_starbucks_date) {
                remaining_time = (valid_duration * 60 * 60 * 1000) - (now.getTime() - rj_starbucks_date);
                console.log('rj_starbucks_remaining_time:'+remaining_time);
                if ( remaining_time > 0 ) {
                    is_valid = true;
                }
            }
        }

        return is_valid;
    };

//test
(function ($) {
$(document).ready(function (e) {
if (typeof window.is_valid_starbucks !== "undefined" ? window.is_valid_starbucks() : false) {

}

       <link href="https://cdn.rawgit.com/h-ibaldo/Raleway_Fixed_Numerals/master/css/rawline.css" rel="stylesheet"/>
       <div class="vertical-banner" style="visibility:hidden;">
        <div class="items">
         <div class="item f-77 set-h">
          <a href="/7at7/?utm_source=article_page&amp;utm_medium=banner&amp;utm_campaign=scrolling">
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="item corona get-h" data-bg="https://res.cloudinary.com/review-journal/image/upload/f_auto,q_auto,c_scale,w_1500/v1596083379/webdev/CORONABANNER.jpg">
          <a href="https://www.reviewjournal.com/news/coronavirus-crisis-1587067663-unique/?utm_campaign=coronavirus&amp;utm_source=lvrj&amp;utm_medium=banner">
           CORONAVIRUS DATA, UPDATED DAILY
          </a>

       <script>
        (function ($) {
    $(document).ready(function (e) {
        var vb_data = {};
        vb_data.headline_duration_time = 2 * 1000; //milli second
        vb_data.headline_transition_time = 1 * 1000;
        vb_data.height = '';
        vb_data.current = 0;
        vb_data.total = 0;
        vb_data.timer_duration;
        vb_data.timer_win_resize;
        vb_data.items_height;
        vb_data.item = [];
    
        setup_vertical_banner();
    
        function setup_vertical_banner() {
            var item, bg;
            $('.vertical-banner .items .item').each(function() {
                if ($(this).attr('data-bg')) {
                    bg = $(this).attr('data-bg');
                    $(this).css('background-image','url("'+bg+'")');
                }
                
            });


            item = $('.vertical-banner .items .item').last().clone();
            $('.vertical-banner .items').prepend(item);
           
            vb_data.total = $('.vertical-banner .items .item').length;
           
            vb_data.current = 1;
            
            
            $('.vertical-banner .item').mouseover(function() {
                if (vb_data.timer_duration) {
                    clearTimeout(vb_data.timer_duration);
                }
            });
    
            $('.vertical-banner .item').mouseout(function() {
                on_duration();
            });
    
            $(window).resize(function(e) {
                if (vb_data.timer_win_resize) {
                    clearTimeout(vb_data.timer_win_resize); 
                }
                vb_data.timer_win_resize = setTimeout(on_win_resize, 200);
            });
    
            //$('.vertical-banner .item:nth-child(0) img').load(function() { 
                vb_data.height = $('.vertical-banner .items .item.get-h').height();
                console.log('rj_hx:'+vb_data.height);
                $('.vertical-banner .item.set-h').css({'height' : vb_data.height+'px'});
                $('.vertical-banner').css({'height' : vb_data.height+'px'});
                $('.vertical-banner').css({'visibility':'visible'});
                //$('.vertical-banner .item.c-2 a').css({'line-height' : vb_data.height+'px'});
                on_duration();
            //});
        }
    
        function on_win_resize() {
            vb_data.height = $('.vertical-banner .items .item.get-h').height();
            $('.vertical-banner .item.set-h').css({'height' : vb_data.height+'px'});
            $('.vertical-banner').css({'height' : vb_data.height+'px'});
            //$('.vertical-banner .item.c-2 a').css({'line-height' : vb_data.height+'px'});
            on_reset();
        }
    
        function on_duration() {
            if (vb_data.timer_duration) {
                clearTimeout(vb_data.timer_duration);
            }
            vb_data.timer_duration = setTimeout(on_transition, vb_data.headline_duration_time);
        }
    
        function on_transition() {
            if (!is_77_enable()) {
               return; 
            }
            
            vb_data.current++;
            var pos = vb_data.height;
            pos = '-='+pos+'px';
            if (vb_data.current < vb_data.total) {
                $('.vertical-banner .items').animate({
                    bottom: pos,
                },vb_data.headline_transition_time, on_duration);
            } else {
                $('.vertical-banner .items').animate({
                    bottom: pos,
                },vb_data.headline_transition_time, on_reset);
            }
        }
        function on_reset() {
            $('.vertical-banner .items').css({'bottom':'0'});
            vb_data.current = 1;
            on_duration();
        }

        function is_77_enable() {
            //las vegas
            //Mon 07:00:00 to Sat 07:00:00
            //utc
            //Mon 14:00:00 to Sat 14:00:00
            //Mon 15:00:00 to Sat 15:00:00;
            var c = new Date();
            var tz = c.getTimezoneOffset(); //420 or 480
            var uday = c.getUTCDay(); //0-6 | Sun-Sat
            var uy = c.getUTCFullYear();
            var um = c.getUTCMonth()+1;
            var ud = c.getUTCDate();
            var uh = c.getUTCHours();
            var ui = c.getUTCMinutes();
            var us = c.getUTCSeconds();
            //console.log('rj_tz: ' + tz);
            //console.log('rj_utc_time: '+ uday+': '+uy+'-'+um+'-'+ud+' '+uh+':'+ui+':'+us);

            hr_limit = 14;
            if (tz == 480) {
                hr_limit = 15;
            }
            if (uday == 0) { //sunday all day
                return false;
            }
            if (uday == 1 && uh < hr_limit) { //monday before 14:00:00
                return false;
            }
            if (uday == 6 && uh >= hr_limit) { //sat after 14:00:00
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        
        }
    });
})(jQuery);
       </script>

       <script>
        (function ($) {
var img_url = 'https://res.cloudinary.com/review-journal/image/upload/f_auto,q_auto,c_scale,w_400/v1611777282/webdev/renee.jpg';
var description = '7 minutes of local non-stop news, free for all users.'
var is_prepend = true;
$(document).ready(function (e) {
    if (is_77_enable() && $('.rj-widget.top-news').length === 1) {

        var u = 'https://spreadsheets.google.com/feeds/list/1jVoUBFY2Xpt9g_eSOhoUipSA_OOh7hMbPDYAqYWx3nI/1/public/values?alt=json';
        $.ajax({
          type: 'GET',
          url: u,
          cache: true,
          dataType: 'json',

                //img_url = response.response.feed.entry[0]['gsx$imageurl']['$t'];
                img_url = response.feed.entry[0]['gsx$imageurl']['$t'];

                console.log('rj_fuel77_img:'+img_url);

            }
          },
          error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
            console.log('_xhr.status:' + xhr.status + '_error:' + thrownError);
          }
        });
    }

    function set_up_77() {
        console.log('rj_set_up_77');
        var current_page = 'not-set';
        if (window.dataLayer[0].metrics.pageType == 'homepage') {
            current_page = 'Homepage';
        }
        if (window.dataLayer[0].metrics.pageType == 'section') {
            current_page = window.dataLayer[0].metrics.name;
        }
        var click_url = '/7at7/?utm_campaign=7at7&utm_medium=topnews_widget&utm_source='+current_page;
        
        if ('Local' == current_page) {
            //is_prepend = false;
        }

        move_story_to_latest();
        
        var sc = document.getElementById('fuel-player-script');
        if(!sc) {
            sc = document.createElement('script');
            sc.type = 'text/javascript';
            sc.src = 'https://fuel-streaming-prod01.fuelmedia.io/player/1.0/player.min.js';
            sc.async = true;
            sc.setAttribute('id', 'fuel-player-script');
            document.head.appendChild(sc); 
        }
        
        var ww = $(window).width();
        var pos = 'mobile';
        if (ww >= 768) {
            pos = 'pc';
        }
        var cls = 'rj-fuel-77';
        if (!is_prepend) {
            cls += ' last-child';
        }

        var fuel =

            .append($('<meta/>',{'itemprop':'name','content':'7@7 FrontPage Channel'}))
            .append($('<meta/>',{'itemprop':'thumbnailUrl','content':img_url}))
            .append($('<meta/>',{'itemprop':'uploadDate','content':'2021-01-18T00:00:00+00:00'}))
            .append($('<meta/>',{'itemprop':'contentUrl','content':'https://fuel-streaming-prod01.fuelmedia.io/v1/sem/877e541a-c3db-43a9-8e84-254cd93da527.m3u8'}))
        ).append(
            $('<div/>',{'class':'f-title'}).append(
                $('<a/>',{'href':click_url, 'alt':'7at7'}).append(
                    $('<span/>',{'html':'Watch '})
                ).append(
                    $('<img/>',{'alt':'logo-7at7','src':'https://res.cloudinary.com/review-journal/image/upload/f_auto,q_auto,c_scale,w_200/v1611100661/webdev/seven2.png'})
                ).append(
                    $('<span/>',{'html':' &mdash;&nbsp; now streaming'})
                )
            )
        ).append(
            $('<div/>',{'class':'f-desc','html':description})
        );
        
        if (ww < 768) {
            fuel.insertBefore('.rj-widget.top-news');
        } else {
            if (is_prepend) {
                fuel.prependTo('.rj-widget.top-news .field-col.left');
            } else {
                fuel.appendTo('.rj-widget.top-news .field-col.left');
            }
        }

        $('.rj-fuel-77 .rj-fuel').append($('<fuel-video/>',{'data-channel':'877e541a-c3db-43a9-8e84-254cd93da527','data-poster-image':img_url}));


        $('.rj-fuel-77 .rj-fuel').on('click touchstart', function(e) {
            if ('undefined' !== typeof s2nVideo) {
                try {
                    s2nVideo.resetPlayer();
                } catch (err) {
                    console.log(err.message);
                }
            }
        });

        /*
        $(window).resize(function(e) {
            check_fuel_bn_position();
        });
        */
    }
    
    function move_story_to_latest() {
        if ($('.latest-news').length < 1) {
            return;
        }
        var elem, tmp, limit;
        limit = 3;
        if ($('.rj-widget.top-news').hasClass('top-news-1-4')) {
        	limit = 4;
        }
        if ($('.rj-widget.top-news .field-col.left .rj-story').length < limit) {
            return;
        }
        elem = $('.rj-widget.top-news .field-col.left .rj-story:last');
        
        if (!elem) {
            return;
        }
        
        elem.addClass('rj-thumb-list');
        elem.wrapInner($('<div>',{'class':'field-col right'}));
        elem.prepend($('<div>',{'class':'field-col left'}));
        tmp = elem.find('.field-col.left');
        elem.find('.field-image').appendTo(tmp);
        elem.insertBefore('.latest-news .rj-story-latest-news-wrap:eq(0)').wrap($('<div>',{'class':'rj-story-latest-news-wrap'}));
    }

    function check_fuel_bn_position() {
        var ww = $(window).width();
        var pos = $('.rj-fuel-77').attr('data-pos');
        if (ww < 768) {
            if ('mobile' !== pos) {
                $('.rj-fuel-77').attr('data-pos', 'mobile');
                $('.rj-fuel-77').insertBefore('.rj-widget.top-news');
            }
        } else {
            if ('pc' !== pos) {
                $('.rj-fuel-77').attr('data-pos', 'pc');
                if (is_prepend) {
                    $('.rj-fuel-77').prependTo('.rj-widget.top-news .field-col.left');
                } else {
                    $('.rj-fuel-77').appendTo('.rj-widget.top-news .field-col.left');
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function is_77_enable() {
        //las vegas
        //Mon 07:00:00 to Sat 07:00:00
        //utc
        //Mon 14:00:00 to Sat 14:00:00
        //Mon 15:00:00 to Sat 15:00:00;
        var c = new Date();
        var tz = c.getTimezoneOffset(); //420 or 480
        var uday = c.getUTCDay(); //0-6 | Sun-Sat
        var uy = c.getUTCFullYear();
        var um = c.getUTCMonth()+1;
        var ud = c.getUTCDate();
        var uh = c.getUTCHours();
        var ui = c.getUTCMinutes();
        var us = c.getUTCSeconds();
        console.log('rj_tz: ' + tz);
        console.log('rj_utc_time: '+ uday+': '+uy+'-'+um+'-'+ud+' '+uh+':'+ui+':'+us);

        hr_limit = 14;
        if (tz == 480) {
            hr_limit = 15;
        }
        if (uday == 0) { //sunday all day
            return false;
        }
        if (uday == 1 && uh < hr_limit) { //monday before 14:00:00
            return false;
        }
        if (uday == 6 && uh >= hr_limit) { //sat after 14:00:00
            return false;
        }
        return true;
        
    }
});
})(jQuery);
       </script>

             Police now required to report more details to FBI on Las Vegas crime
            </a>
           </div>

             </span>

              March 21, 2021 - 7:22 am
             </time>
             <time class="entry-date updated" datetime="">
              March 21, 2021 - 7:22 am
             </time>
            </div>

           <div class="field-excerpt">
            <p>
             An FBI mandate that took effect in January overhauled the way police agencies across the country report crime data, and local police are expecting it will project a rise in crime.
            </p>

        <div class="textwidget">
         <div class="rj-scroll-lock" data-end-elem="#rj-region-sidebar-1" data-top="100">
          <div style="min-height:320px;">
           <div class="rj-ads-wrapper" style="overflow:visible;">
            <div id="ad-sidebar_1">
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>

       <div class="rj-widget-num-4 rj-widget-last rj-widget-even rj-widget rj_widget_text" id="rj_widget_text-367">
        <div class="textwidget">
         <script>
          (function ($) {
      $(document).ready(function (e) {
         
         var scroll_lock_cont = $('<div>',{'class':'rj-scroll-lock-cont lock-disabled'});
         $('.rj-scroll-lock').wrap(scroll_lock_cont);

         var scroll_lock;
         var end_elem;
         var end_elem_selector;

         var pos_lock_top;
         var pos_lock_end = 0;
         var end_elem_top;
         var end_elem_height;

         var scroll_lock_top;
         var scroll_lock_width;
         var scroll_lock_height;

         var scroll_lock_cont_top;
         
         var has_admin_bar = false;
         if ($('body').hasClass('admin-bar')) {
            has_admin_bar = true;
         }
        

         $('.rj-scroll-lock').each(function() {
            scroll_lock = $(this);
            scroll_lock_cont = $(scroll_lock).closest('.rj-scroll-lock-cont');
            pos_lock_top = 0;
           
            pos_lock_top = parseInt(scroll_lock.attr('data-top'));
            if (has_admin_bar) {
               pos_lock_top = pos_lock_top + 32;
            }
            scroll_lock.attr('data-lock-top',pos_lock_top);
            scroll_lock_width = scroll_lock.width(); //scroll_lock.children().outerWidth(true);
            scroll_lock_height = scroll_lock.height(); //scroll_lock.children().outerHeight(true);

           
            scroll_lock.css({'top':pos_lock_top+'px','height':scroll_lock_height+'px'}); //'width':scroll_lock_width+'px',
            scroll_lock_cont.css({'height':scroll_lock_height+'px'}); //'width':scroll_lock_width+'px',

         });

        
         $(window).on('scroll resize', function() {
            //console.log('w_sc_top:'+$(window).scrollTop());
            if ($(window).width() < 1100) {
               $('.rj-scroll-lock-cont').addClass('lock-disabled');
               return;
            } else {
               $('.rj-scroll-lock-cont').removeClass('lock-disabled');
            }

           
            
            $('.rj-scroll-lock').each(function() {
               scroll_lock = $(this);
               scroll_lock_cont = scroll_lock.closest('.rj-scroll-lock-cont');

               end_elem_selector = scroll_lock.attr('data-end-elem');
               end_elem = $(end_elem_selector);

                end_elem_top = end_elem.offset().top;
                end_elem_height = end_elem.outerHeight();

               scroll_lock_cont_top = scroll_lock_cont.offset().top;
               scroll_lock_height = scroll_lock.height();
               
               pos_lock_top = scroll_lock.attr('data-lock-top');
               pos_lock_top = parseInt(pos_lock_top);
               pos_lock_end = end_elem_top + end_elem_height - pos_lock_top - scroll_lock_height;

//console.log('sctop:'+$(window).scrollTop());
//console.log('pos_lock_end:'+pos_lock_end);

               if ( ($(window).scrollTop() > (scroll_lock_cont_top-pos_lock_top)) && ($(window).scrollTop() < pos_lock_end) ) {
                  scroll_lock_cont.addClass('lock-enabled');
               } else {
                  scroll_lock_cont.removeClass('lock-enabled');
               }
            });
            
         });
      });
   })(jQuery);
         </script>
         <style>
          .rj-scroll-lock {
   position: static;
   z-index: 2;
}
.rj-scroll-lock-cont.lock-enabled .rj-scroll-lock {
   position: fixed;
} 
.rj-scroll-lock-cont.lock-disabled {
   width: auto !important;
   height: auto !important;
}
.rj-scroll-lock-cont.lock-disabled .rj-scroll-lock {
   position: static;
   width: auto !important;
   height: auto !important;
}
         </style>

       <div class="rj-widget-num-2 rj-widget-even rj-widget rj_widget_text" id="rj_widget_text-376">
        <div class="textwidget">
         <div class="rj-widget default podcast rj-gutter-mobile" data-podcast-id="1,2,3,4,5,7,9" data-render-num="1">
         </div>
         <div class="separator-horizontal">
         </div>
         <script>
          (function ($) {
   //$(document).ready(function (e) {
        window.rj_podcast = window.rj_podcast || {};
        window.rj_podcast.mobbedup = {
          'title': 'Mobbed Up: The Fight for Las Vegas',
          'description': 'The true-crime series chronicles the mob’s rise and fall in Las Vegas through the eyes of those who lived it.',
          'image': 'https://res.cloudinary.com/review-journal/image/upload/f_auto,q_auto,c_scale,w_100/v1588965207/webdev/MOBBEDUPwithlogos.jpg',
          'url': 'https://www.reviewjournal.com/podcasts/#MobbedUp!'
        };
        window.rj_podcast.domain = '';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_url = '/podcasts';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name = [];
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name['1'] = 'Vegas Nation';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name['2'] = 'Golden Edge';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name['3'] = 'ringside';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name['4'] = 'PodKats!';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name['5'] = 'Rebels in Ruins';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name['7'] = 'RJ Politics';
        window.rj_podcast.podcast_name['9'] = 'One October';
        window.rj_podcast.cache_data = [];
        
        setup_widget();
        
        function setup_widget() {
            $('.rj-widget.podcast').each(function() {
                get_data(this);
            });
        }

        function get_data(elem) {
            var podcast_id, pod_id, link, i, cls, data;
            podcast_id_all = $(elem).attr('data-podcast-id');
            
            $(elem).append(
               $('<div/>',{'class':'rj-widget-title','html':'PODCASTS'}))
            .append(
               $('<div/>',{'class':'field-list'}))
            .append(
               $('<div/>',{'class':'field-more-small'}).append(
                  $('<a/>',{'href':window.rj_podcast.domain + window.rj_podcast.podcast_url, 'text':'MORE EPISODES'})
               )
            );

            link = window.rj_podcast.domain + '/wp-json/rj/v2/api?name=project&end_point=/podcasts/latest-json?id=' +podcast_id_all;
           
            $.ajax({
              type: 'GET',
              url: link,
              cache: true,
              dataType: 'json',
              success: function (response) {
                if ( response.status == '1' && typeof(response.response) !== 'undefined') {
                  //podcast_loaded++;
                  data = response.response;
                  for (i=0; i<data.length; i++) {
                    pod_id = data[i].id;
                    window.rj_podcast.cache_data[pod_id] = data[i];
                  }
                  render_data(elem);
                }
                 
              },
              error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                console.log('_xhr.status:' + xhr.status + '_error:' + thrownError);
              }
            });
        }

        function render_data(elem) {
          var podcast_id, i, pod_sort, latest_pubdate, render_num, episode, url, cover;
          podcast_id = $(elem).attr('data-podcast-id');
          podcast_id = podcast_id.split(',');
          render_num = $(elem).attr('data-render-num');
          pod_sort = [];
          for (i=0; i<podcast_id.length; i++) {
            if (typeof window.rj_podcast.cache_data[podcast_id[i]] != 'undefined') {
              latest_pubdate = window.rj_podcast.cache_data[podcast_id[i]].episodes[0].pubdate
              //console.log('b: '+podcast_id[i] +'_' +latest_pubdate);
              pod_sort.push({'id':podcast_id[i],'latest_pubdate':latest_pubdate});
            } 
          }

          pod_sort.sort(
            function(a, b) {
              if (a.latest_pubdate < b.latest_pubdate) {
                return 1;
              }
              return -1;
            }
          );

          if (pod_sort.length < render_num) {
            render_num = pod_sort.length;
          }

          var txt;
          for (i=0; i<render_num; i++) {
            episode = window.rj_podcast.cache_data[pod_sort[i].id].episodes[0];
            txt = episode.title+'&nbsp; <span style="color:#777;">'+episode.about+'</span>';
            url = window.rj_podcast.domain + window.rj_podcast.podcast_url+'/#'+window.rj_podcast.podcast_name[pod_sort[i].id];
            cover = resize_image(episode.cover, 'f_auto,q_auto,c_scale,w_100');

            $(elem).find('.field-list').append($('<div/>',{'class':'rj-podcast','data-podcast-id':pod_sort[i].id,'data-latest-pubdate':pod_sort[i].latest_pubdate})
              .append($('<div/>',{'class':'field-image'})
                .append($('<a/>',{'href':url})
                  .append($('<img/>',{'class':'field-img rj-lazy-load lazy-image', 'src':cover, 'alt':'podcast '+pod_sort[i].id, 'data-lazy-src':cover, 'srcset':'data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7'}))
                  .append($('<div/>',{'class':'play-button pb-bot-left'}))
                )
              )
              .append($('<div/>',{'class':'field-info'})
                .append($('<div/>',{'class':'field-title'})
                  .append($('<a/>',{'href':url,'html':txt}))
                )
              )
            );
          }

          if (typeof(window.rj_podcast.mobbedup) != 'undefined')  {
            url = window.rj_podcast.mobbedup.url;
            cover = window.rj_podcast.mobbedup.image;
            txt = window.rj_podcast.mobbedup.title+'&nbsp; <span style="color:#777;">'+window.rj_podcast.mobbedup.description+'</span>';
            $(elem).find('.field-list').prepend($('<div/>',{'class':'rj-podcast'})
              .append($('<div/>',{'class':'field-image'})
                .append($('<a/>',{'href':url})
                  .append($('<img/>',{'class':'field-img rj-lazy-load lazy-image', 'src':cover, 'alt':'podcast mobbedup', 'data-lazy-src':cover, 'srcset':'data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7'}))
                  .append($('<div/>',{'class':'play-button pb-bot-left'}))
                )
              )
              .append($('<div/>',{'class':'field-info'})
                .append($('<div/>',{'class':'field-title'})
                  .append($('<a/>',{'href':url,'html':txt}))
                )
              )
            );
          }
          //$(elem).addClass('ready');
          //$(document.body).trigger('post-load', {});
        }

        function resize_image(img_url, resize_str) {
            if (img_url.indexOf('res.cloudinary.com') > -1) {
               img_url = img_url.replace('/image/upload/v', '/image/upload/'+resize_str+'/v');
            }
            return img_url;
        }

    //});
    })(jQuery);
         </script>
         <style>
          .rj-podcast .field-title {
    display: -webkit-box;
    -webkit-line-clamp: 5;
    -webkit-box-orient: vertical;
    overflow: hidden;
}
         </style>
        </div>
       </div>

        (function(userDB) {
        var initialized;
        var done = function () {
            if (!initialized) {
                initialized = true;
                timerId && clearTimeout(timerId);

                if (window.Connext && window.Connext.Run) {
                    window.Connext.Run();

                } else {
                    // wait for Connext to load
                    var timerIdPoll = setInterval(function () {
                        if (window.Connext && window.Connext.Run) {
                            clearInterval(timerIdPoll);
                            window.Connext.Run();
                        }
                    }, 500);
                }
            }
        };
        var timerId = setTimeout(function () {
            done();
        }, 3000);

            tracker.setPaywall('mg2');
            if (userDB) {

                });

                done();

function set_onesignal_ext_id(ext_id) {
  if ('undefined' == typeof(Storage) || 'undefined' == typeof(OneSignal)) {
    return;
  }
  if (ext_id != localStorage.set_onesignal_ext_id) {
    localStorage.set_onesignal_ext_id = ext_id;
    OneSignal.push(function() {
        OneSignal.setExternalUserId(ext_id);
    });
    $('#rj_widget_text-349 > .textwidget:eq(0)').append('<p>'+ext_id+'</p>');
  }
}

       <script>
        (function ($) {
$(document).ready(function (e) {
    $('.nlsm-widget .btn-signup').click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var nwrapper = $(this).parent().parent();
        if (nwrapper.length === 0) {
            return;
        }
        var pref_id = nwrapper.attr('data-prefid');
        var user_email = nwrapper.find('.user-email').val();
        var err_elem = nwrapper.find('.err-msg');
        if (!pref_id) {
            err_elem.text('Missing settings!');
            return;
        }
        if (!user_email) {
            err_elem.text('Email is required!');
            return;
        }

        if (!rj_validate_email(user_email)) {
            err_elem.text('Invalid Email address!');
            return;
        }
        
        pref_id = pref_id.split(',');
        set_email_pref(user_email, nwrapper, pref_id, err_elem);        
    });

    function rj_validate_email(email) {
        return /^\w+([\.-]?\w+)*@\w+([\.-]?\w+)*(\.\w{2,3})+$/.test(email);
    }

    function set_email_pref(user_email, nwrapper, pref_id, err_elem) {
        var url = '/wp-json/rj/v2/api?name=newsletters';
        url += '&end_point=/userpreferences/';
        url += '&headers=' + encodeURIComponent('Content-Type=application/json');
        url += '&method=POST';
        //var body = '{"User":{"email":"'+user_email+'"},"EmailPreferences":[{"EmailPreferenceId":'+pref_id+',"Selected":1}]}';

        var pref_id_str = [];
        for (var i=0; i<pref_id.length; i++) {
            pref_id_str[i] = '{"EmailPreferenceId":'+pref_id[i]+',"Selected":1}';
        }

        var body = '{"User":{"email":"'+user_email+'"},"EmailPreferences":[' + pref_id_str.join(',') + ']}';
       
        url += '&body=' + encodeURIComponent(body);
        err_elem.html('&nbsp;');
        $.ajax({
            'method':'GET',
            'dataType': 'json',
            'cache': false,
            'url': url,
            'success': function (response) {
                if (response.status == '1' && response.response) {
                    if (response.response.Code && response.response.Code == '200') {
                        err_elem.text('Thank you');
                        mather_event_complete(user_email, nwrapper, pref_id)
                    } else {
                        if (response.response.Errors[0].Message) {
                            err_elem.text('Oops something went wrong '+response.response.Errors[0].Message);
                        } else {
                            err_elem.text('Oops something went wrong, please try again later'); 
                        }
                    }        
                } else {
                    err_elem.text('Oops something went wrong '+response.response);
                }
            },
            'error': function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                console.log('_xhr.status:' + xhr.status + '_error:' + thrownError);
                err_elem.text('Oops something went wrong, please try again later');
            }
        });
    }

    function mather_event_complete(user_email, nwrapper, pref_id) {
        var title = nwrapper.find('.rj-widget-title').text();
        var offers = [];
        for (var i=0; i<pref_id.length; i++) {
           offers.push({"offerName":title, "offerId": pref_id[i], "campaign": "News Blast"});
        }

        var event_obj = {"action": "signup_completed", "offers": offers};
        var options = {"email": user_email};
        mather_send_event(event_obj, options);
    }

    function mather_send_event(event_obj, options) {
        console.log('matherq');
        var m = ['newsletterEvent', event_obj, options];
        console.log(m);
        (window._matherq = window._matherq || []).push(m);
    }
});
})(jQuery);
       </script>

       <script>
        (function ($) {
    $(document).ready(function (e) {
        if (window.localStorage) {
            check_storage();    
        } else {
            check_cookie();
        }
        
        function check_storage() {
            var is_accept_cookie = getCookie('is_accept_cookie');
            console.log('rj_cookie:'+is_accept_cookie);
            if (is_accept_cookie == '1') {
                return;   
            }

            current_date = new Date().getTime();
            current_date = current_date / (1000); //24*60*60*
            current_date = parseInt(current_date);
            
            $('.accept-cookie .field-btn').click(function() {
                window.localStorage.setItem('rj_cookie_date', current_date);
                window.localStorage.setItem('rj_cookie_diff', (365*24*60*60));
                $('.accept-cookie').hide();
            });
            
            $('.accept-cookie .x-btn').click(function() {
                window.localStorage.setItem('rj_cookie_date', current_date);
                window.localStorage.setItem('rj_cookie_diff', (1*24*60*60));
                $('.accept-cookie').hide();
            });
                
            var rj_cookie_date = window.localStorage.getItem('rj_cookie_date');
            rj_cookie_date = parseInt(rj_cookie_date);
            if (!Number.isInteger(rj_cookie_date)) {
                rj_cookie_date = 0;
            }
            
            var rj_cookie_diff = window.localStorage.getItem('rj_cookie_diff');
            rj_cookie_diff = parseInt(rj_cookie_diff);
            console.log('rj_cookie_diff:'+rj_cookie_diff);
            if (rj_cookie_diff != (365*24*60*60)) {
                rj_cookie_diff = (1*24*60*60);
            }
    
            var date_diff = current_date - rj_cookie_date;
            console.log('rj_cookie_diff:'+ rj_cookie_diff);
            var dd = date_diff/86400;
            dd = dd.toFixed(2);
            console.log('rj_cookie_date:'+dd );
            if (dd > 5) {
                dd = 5;
            }
            //$('.powered-by').append(dd);
            //$('.powered-by').append('<div>'+date_diff+'|'+rj_cookie_diff+'</div>');

            if (date_diff >= rj_cookie_diff) {
                $('.accept-cookie').show(); 
            }
        }
        
        function check_cookie() {
            $('.accept-cookie .field-btn').bind('click', accept_cookie);
            $('.accept-cookie .x-btn').bind('click', x_btn_clicked);
        
            var is_accept_cookie = getCookie('is_accept_cookie');
            if (is_accept_cookie != '1' && is_accept_cookie != '0') {
                $('.accept-cookie').show();    
            } 
        }
        
        function x_btn_clicked() {
            setCookie('is_accept_cookie', '0', 1); //1year = 365, 10 mins = 0.007
            $('.accept-cookie').hide();
        }

        function accept_cookie() {
            setCookie('is_accept_cookie', '1', 365); //1year = 365, 10 mins = 0.007
            $('.accept-cookie').hide();
        }
        function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
            var d = new Date();
            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            var expires = 'expires='+d.toUTCString();
            document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';' + expires + ';path=/';
        }
        function getCookie(a) {
            var b = document.cookie.match('(^|[^;]+)\\s*' + a + '\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)');
            return b ? b.pop() : '';
        }
    });
})(jQuery);
       </script>

       <script>
        (function ($) {
  $(document).ready(function (e) {
    if (!window.localStorage) {
      return;
    }

    var current_date = new Date().getTime();
    current_date = current_date / (1000); //24*60*60*
    current_date = parseInt(current_date);

    var rj_newsletter_date = window.localStorage.getItem('rj_newsletter_date');
    rj_newsletter_date = parseInt(rj_newsletter_date);
    if (!Number.isInteger(rj_newsletter_date)) {
      rj_newsletter_date = 0;
    }

    var rj_newsletter_th = window.localStorage.getItem('rj_newsletter_th');
    rj_newsletter_th = parseInt(rj_newsletter_th);
    if (!Number.isInteger(rj_newsletter_th)) {
      rj_newsletter_th = 0;
    }
    rj_newsletter_th++;

    var date_diff = current_date - rj_newsletter_date;
   
    console.log('rj_nl_current_date:'+current_date);
    console.log('rj_nl_date:'+rj_newsletter_date);
    console.log('rj_nl_th:'+rj_newsletter_th);
    console.log('rj_nl_date_diff:'+date_diff);

    if (date_diff >= (14*24*60*60) && rj_newsletter_th <=2) {
        window.localStorage.setItem('rj_newsletter_th', rj_newsletter_th);
        setTimeout(function() {
          $('.signup-box').show();  
        }, 10000);  
    } 
    function hide_signup_box() {
      window.localStorage.setItem('rj_newsletter_date', current_date);
      $('.signup-box').hide();
    }

    $('.signup-box').click(function(e) {
      if (e.target === this) {
        hide_signup_box();
      }
    });

    $('.signup-box .f-close').click(function(e) {
      hide_signup_box();
    });

    $('.signup-box .f-signup').click(function(e) {
      var signup_box = $(e.target).closest('.signup-box');
      var user_email =  signup_box.find('.user-email').val();
      var msg_elem = signup_box.find('.f-msg');
       
      $('.signup-box .f-msg').html('&nbsp;');

      var pref_id = [];
      $('.signup-box .f-checkbox input:checked').each(function() {
          pref_id.push($(this).val());
      });

      if (!user_email) {
          msg_elem.text('please fill in your email address');
          return;
      }
      if (pref_id.length < 1) {
          msg_elem.text('please check at least one newsletter');
          return;
      }
      console.log('user_email:'+ user_email);
      console.log('pref_id:'+pref_id);
      set_email_pref(user_email, pref_id); 
    });

    $('.signup-box .f-manage').click(function(e) {
      var signup_box = $(e.target).closest('.signup-box');
      var user_email =  signup_box.find('.user-email').val();
      var url = 'https://www.reviewjournal.com/email-alerts/?manage=1';
      if (user_email) {
        url += '&email='+user_email;
      }
      window.location.href = url;
    });

    function set_email_pref(user_email, pref_id) {
        var url = '/wp-json/rj/v2/api?name=newsletters';
        url += '&end_point=/userpreferences/';
        url += '&headers=' + encodeURIComponent('Content-Type=application/json');
        url += '&method=POST';
        //var body = '{"User":{"email":"'+user_email+'"},"EmailPreferences":[{"EmailPreferenceId":'+pref_id+',"Selected":1}]}';

        var pref_id_str = [];
        for (var i=0; i<pref_id.length; i++) {
            pref_id_str[i] = '{"EmailPreferenceId":'+pref_id[i]+',"Selected":1}';
        }

        var body = '{"User":{"email":"'+user_email+'"},"EmailPreferences":[' + pref_id_str.join(',') + ']}';
       
        url += '&body=' + encodeURIComponent(body);
        $('.signup-box .f-msg').html('&nbsp;');
        $.ajax({
            'method':'GET',
            'dataType': 'json',
            'cache': false,
            'url': url,
            'success': function (response) {
                if (response.status == '1' && response.response) {
                    if (response.response.Code && response.response.Code == '200') {
                        $('.signup-box .f-msg').text('Thank you');
                        setTimeout(function() {
                          window.localStorage.setItem('rj_newsletter_th', 100);
                          hide_signup_box();
                        }, 1000);
                    } else {
                        if (response.response.Errors[0].Message) {
                            $('.signup-box .f-msg').text('Oops something went wrong '+response.response.Errors[0].Message);
                        } else {
                            $('.signup-box .f-msg').text('Oops something went wrong, please try again later'); 
                        }
                    }        
                } else {
                    $('.signup-box .f-msg').text('Oops something went wrong '+response.response);
                }
            },
            'error': function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                console.log('_xhr.status:' + xhr.status + '_error:' + thrownError);
                $('.signup-box .f-msg').text('Oops something went wrong, please try again later');
            }
        });
    }

    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
      var d = new Date();
      d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
      var expires = 'expires='+d.toUTCString();
      document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';' + expires + ';path=/';
    }
    function getCookie(a) {
      var b = document.cookie.match('(^|[^;]+)\\s*' + a + '\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)');
      return b ? b.pop() : '';
    }

  });
})(jQuery);
       </script>

  <script>
   var parselyPreload = {eventQueue: [], loaded: false};

                function fireParselyEvent(event) {
                    if (parselyPreload.loaded) {
                        PARSELY.beacon.trackPageView(event);
                    } else {
                        parselyPreload.eventQueue.push(event);
                    }
                }

                // when Parse.ly is done loading, flush the queue
                window.PARSELY = {
                    onload: function () {
                        console.log("Parse.ly code has loaded!");
                        parselyPreload.loaded = true;
                        for (var i = 0; i < parselyPreload.eventQueue.length; i++) {
                            PARSELY.beacon.trackPageView(parselyPreload.eventQueue[i]);
                        }
                    }
                };

				
                PARSELY.autotrack = false;
                PARSELY.onReady = function () {
                    console.log("Parse.ly code is ready!");
                    getSubscriberInfo();
                };

                window.rjConnext = {
                    init: false,
                    done: false,
                    viewed: false,
                    getUserState: function() {
                        if (window.Connext && window.Connext.Storage && window.Connext.Storage.GetUserState) {
                            return window.Connext.Storage.GetUserState();
                        }
                        return null;
                    },
                    isReady: function() {
                        return window.rjConnext.done && !window.rjConnext.viewed;
                    },
                    onFinish: function(e) {
                        window.rjConnext.done = true;
                    },
                    complete: function() {
                        window.rjConnext.init = true;
                        window.rjConnext.done = true;
                        window.rjConnext.viewed = true;
                    }
                };

                document.addEventListener("onFinish", function(e) {
                    console.log("Parse.ly EventListener: onFinish.", e);
                    window.rjConnext.onFinish(e);
                });

                function getSubscriberInfo() {
                    if (window.rjConnext.init) {
                        return;
                    }
                    window.rjConnext.init = true;
                    if (window.rjConnext.isReady()) {
                        parselyTrackAudienceSegments(window.rjConnext.getUserState());
                    } else {
                        // wait for Connext to load (no more than 10 seconds)
                        var try_max = 20, try_count = 0;
                        var try_timer = setInterval(function () {
                            try_count++;
                            if (try_count < try_max) {
                                if (window.rjConnext.isReady()) {
                                    clearInterval(try_timer);
                                    parselyTrackAudienceSegments(window.rjConnext.getUserState());
                                }
                            } else {
                                clearInterval(try_timer);
                                parselyTrackAudienceSegments(null);
                            }
                        }, 500);
                    }
                }

                function parselyTrackAudienceSegments(subscription) {
                    window.rjConnext.complete();
                    console.log('Parse.ly Track Audience', subscription);
                    PARSELY.updateDefaults({
                        data: {
                            plan: subscription
                        }
                    });
                    PARSELY.beacon.trackPageView();
                }
  </script>
